0                                   2009      77.              COPY  SLISTMAC
                                    2010             =*******************************************************************
                                    2011             =*                                                                 *
                                    2012             =* Macros for the serialized manipulation of single linked lists   *
                                    2013             =* in memory.  These lists are of the PUSH/POP (LIFO) variety.     *
                                    2014             =* Serialization is achieved using the CDS and CS instructions.    *
                                    2015             =*                                                                 *
                                    2016             =*******************************************************************
0                                   2018             =*******************************************************************
                                    2019             =*                                                                 *
                                    2020             =* Single linked list head fields                                  *
                                    2021             =*                                                                 *
                                    2022             =*******************************************************************
                                    2023             =         MACRO
                                    2024             =&LAB     SHEAD
                                    2025             =         AIF   ('&LAB' EQ '').ERR
                                    2026             =&LAB     DS   0D                   Single linked CDS list
                                    2027             =&LAB.FP  DS    A                   Forward pointer
                                    2028             =&LAB.SEQ DS    A                   CDS sequence number
                                    2029             =         MEXIT
                                    2030             =.ERR     MNOTE 8,'Label (list name) required'
                                    2031             =         MEND
0                                   2033             =*******************************************************************
                                    2034             =*                                                                 *
                                    2035             =* Push an item onto a single linked list                          *
                                    2036             =*                                                                 *
                                    2037             =*******************************************************************
                                    2038             =         MACRO
                                    2039             =&LABEL   SPUSH &HEAD=,&ITEM=
                                    2040             =         LCLC  &X
                                    2041             =         AIF   ('&LABEL' EQ '').NOLAB
                                    2042             =&LABEL   LABEL ,
                                    2043             =.NOLAB   ANOP  ,
                                    2044             =         AIF   ('&HEAD' EQ '').ERR1
                                    2045             =         AIF   ('&ITEM' EQ '').ERR2
                                    2047             =         LM    R14,R15,&HEAD       Get fwd ptr and sequence number
                                    2048             =         LA    RVR,&ITEM           Point to new item
                                    2049             =         LOOP  BEGIN
                                    2050             =         LA    RS,1(R15)           Increment sequence
                                    2051             =         MVC   &ITEM.(L'&HEAD.FP),&HEAD.FP Set item fwd ptr
                                    2052             =         CDS   R14,RVR,&HEAD       Add item to list
                                    2053             =         UNTIL (Z),END
                                    2055             =         AGO   .EXIT
                                    2056             =.ERR1    MNOTE 8,'Head is a required parameter'
                                    2057             =         AGO   .EXIT
                                    2058             =.ERR2    MNOTE 8,'Item is a required parameter'
                                    2059             =.EXIT    ANOP  ,
                                    2060             =         MEND  ,
0                                   2062             =*******************************************************************
                                    2063             =*                                                                 *
                                    2064             =* Pop an item from a single linked list. Addr returned in RVR     *
                                    2065             =* (zero if the list was empty).                                   *
                                    2066             =*                                                                 *
1VSSV     (VSSV07) (09:49) (22MAR04) ORVYL'S INTERNAL SET, SHOW AND DUMP COMMANDS                                           Page   15

0                                   2067             =*******************************************************************
                                    2068             =         MACRO
                                    2069             =&LABEL   SPOP  &HEAD=
                                    2070             =         AIF   ('&LABEL' EQ '').NOLAB
                                    2071             =&LABEL   LABEL ,
                                    2072             =.NOLAB   ANOP  ,
                                    2073             =         AIF   ('&HEAD' EQ '').ERR1
                                    2075             =         LM    RVR,RS,&HEAD        Get fwd and sequence number
                                    2076             =         LOOP  BEGIN
                                    2077             =         IF    (RVR,Z),EXIT        None to get
                                    2078             =         LR    R14,RVR             Point to first item
                                    2079             =         L     R14,0(R14)          Get fwd pointer
                                    2080             =         LA    R15,1(RS)           Increment sequence
                                    2081             =         CDS   RVR,R14,&HEAD       Remove item from list
                                    2082             =         UNTIL (Z),END
                                    2084             =         AGO   .EXIT
                                    2085             =.ERR1    MNOTE 8,'Head is a required parameter'
                                    2086             =.EXIT    ANOP  ,
                                    2087             =         MEND  ,
0                                   2089             =*******************************************************************
                                    2090             =*                                                                 *
                                    2091             =* Get an available item from list (ptr returned in RVR). Memory   *
                                    2092             =* will be obtained if the list is empty.                          *
                                    2093             =*                                                                 *
                                    2094             =*******************************************************************
                                    2095             =         MACRO
                                    2096             =&LABEL   SAVAIL &HEAD=,&LEN=,&LOC=GLOBHI,&FIX=,&PAGE=
                                    2097             =         AIF   ('&LABEL' EQ '').NOLAB
                                    2098             =&LABEL   LABEL ,
                                    2099             =.NOLAB   ANOP  ,
                                    2100             =         AIF   ('&HEAD' EQ '').ERR1
                                    2101             =         AIF   ('&LEN' EQ '').ERR2
                                    2102             =         SPOP  HEAD=&HEAD          pop a free item
                                    2103             =         IF    (RVR,Z),BEGIN       empty list
                                    2104             =         VMGET &LEN,LOC=&LOC,FIX=&FIX,PAGE=&PAGE
                                    2105             =         IF    ('LTR RVR,RVR',ZERO),'ABORT NO_MEM_&HEAD'
                                    2106             =         END   ,
                                    2107             =         AGO   .EXIT
                                    2108             =.ERR1    MNOTE 8,'Head is a required parameter'
                                    2109             =         AGO   .EXIT
                                    2110             =.ERR2    MNOTE 8,'Len is a required parameter'
                                    2111             =.EXIT    ANOP  ,
                                    2112             =         MEND  ,
